          THE STORAGE AREA (IN STATIC) FOR THE PROCEDURE LABELLED CLEAR_OUTPUT IS 168 BYTES LONG.

                     /*****************************************************************/      119
     5                   PUT SKIP LIST('STARTING TTYPLI USING ',WS_MODULE_NAME1);              21
     6                   PUT SKIP;  /* FORCE STREAM IO BUFFER TO FLUSH. OTHERWISE              22
                                       PREVIOUS PUT WILL NOT SHOW UNTIL AFTER                  22
                                       FULL SCREEN OPERATIONS END */                           22
                                                                                               24
     7                   TTY_FUNC = TTYFUNC_STRT;                                              25
     8                   CALL CALL_3270_IO;                                                    26
                                                                                               27
     9                   TTY_LINE_OUT = 'HELLO WORLD';                                         28
    10                   TTY_LINE_IN  = '>';                                                   29
    11                   TTY_ERR_MSG  = ' ';                                                   30
